   Location: /home/blue/PyPIAgent/Dataset/study/unzip_benign/colour_science-0.4.6/colour_science-0.4.6/colour/notation/datasets/munsell/__init__.py:23
   More Info: https://bandit.readthedocs.io/en/latest/plugins/b824_url_found.html
22	)
23	MUNSELL_COLOURS.__doc__ = """
24	Define the *Munsell Renotation System* datasets.
25	
26	-   ``Munsell Colours All``: *all* published *Munsell* colours, including the
27	    extrapolated colors.
28	-   ``Munsell Colours 1929``: the colours appearing in the 1929
29	    *Munsell Book of Color*. These data has been used in the scaling
30	    experiments leading to the 1943 renotation.
31	-   ``Munsell Colours Real``: *real*, within MacAdam limits *Munsell* colours
32	    only. They are the colours listed in the original 1943 renotation article
33	    *(Newhall, Nickerson, & Judd, 1943)*.
34	
35	Notes
36	-----
37	-   The Munsell Renotation data commonly available within the *all.dat*,
38	    *experimental.dat* and *real.dat* files features *CIE xyY* colourspace
39	    values that are scaled by a :math:`1 / 0.975 \\simeq 1.02568` factor. If
40	    you are performing conversions using *Munsell* *Colorlab* specification,
41	    e.g., *2.5R 9/2*, according to *ASTM D1535-08e1* method, you should not
42	    scale the output :math:`Y` Luminance. However, if you use directly the
43	    *CIE xyY* colourspace values from the Munsell Renotation data, you should
44	    scale the :math:`Y` Luminance before conversions by a :math:`0.975` factor.
45	
46	    *ASTM D1535-08e1* states that::
47	
48	        The coefficients of this equation are obtained from the 1943 equation
49	        by multiplying each coefficient by 0.975, the reflectance factor of
50	        magnesium oxide with respect to the perfect reflecting diffuser, and
51	        rounding to ve digits of precision.
52	
53	-   Chromaticities assume *CIE Illuminant C*, approximately 6700K, as neutral
54	    origin for both the hue and chroma loci.
55	
56	References
57	----------
58	-   :cite:`MunsellColorSciencec` : Munsell Color Science. (n.d.). Munsell
59	    Colours Data. Retrieved August 20, 2014, from
60	    http://www.cis.rit.edu/research/mcsl2/online/munsell.php
61	
62	Aliases:
63	
64	-   'all': 'Munsell Colours All'
65	-   '1929': 'Munsell Colours 1929'
66	-   'real': 'Munsell Colours Real'
67	"""
68	MUNSELL_COLOURS["all"] = MUNSELL_COLOURS["Munsell Colours All"]
